It trims so well and so short that I don't need to use it as much as my old rotary trimmer. I wash it every time I use it (because it says to do it) with warm water while it's running, then while it's stopped, and then once more with it running again. This is probably overkill, but I like to be thorough. I see some complaints in the reviews which I am almost certain are related to being too lazy to wash it after using it. So, I'm thinking, this is something you put in an area where mucous membranes are and if mucous gets on something and is allowed to dry, it hardens. It can almost be glue like. So, the trimmer blades get covered in a glue like substance from your nose, you don't clean it, and the blades stop moving. Please tell me that you're not surprised, and please tell me you don't blame the product. What do you expect? Norelco tells you to wash it after you use it. There might be a reason why! Auto manufacturers tell you to change the oil in your car. What do you think is going to happen if you never do, or do it poorly? Bottom line, product works exceedingly well - and for some of the doubters or people who don't like it because they can't follow instructions, let me add this caveat: \\"It works extremely well when used as directed.\\" I am sure there are a couple of issues every now and again. Six sigma (which I'm sure Norelco tries to apply as they are big enough to do so) is only so good when it comes to quality control, so a rare lemon is to be expected. But considering that there are several negative reviews out of only 119, I'm sure intelligence or ability to follow directions has come into play - at least to a certain extent. I'm no rocket scientist, but it doesn't take a genius to come to that conclusion. If the functionality ever changes within the next few years, I will update this review, but I have no reason to expect that it will. Additionally, if I can remember to do so, I will try to give an estimate of battery life after the time comes when I need to replace the original battery. It may not mean a whole lot as people use it differently and at different frequencies and for different durations, but at least it will give you a data point. December 2013 - It's still perfect.
